<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opvanghuis.html>opvanghuis</a> (22144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opvangen.html>opvangen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shelter, to temporarily house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opvoeren.html>opvoeren</a> (9764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:opvoeren.html>opvoeren</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeren.html>voeren</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opvoeren.html>opvoeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to perform (e.g. a play or <a href = vnd.unilang:opera.html>opera</a>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> automotive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to soup up, to tune up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to increase, to intensify</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to raise, to <a href = vnd.unilang:lift.html>lift</a> up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exalt, to elate</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wind</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wind, draft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Aufwind</i>.
</p>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opwinden.html>opwinden</a> (12444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:opwinden.html>opwinden</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:winden.html>winden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opwinden.html>opwinden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To wind, to wind up; e.g. to tighten a clockwork mechanism</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To agitate, to excite</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To get agitated, to get excited, to become aggravated</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opwindend.html>opwindend</a> (3871)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opwindend.html>opwindend</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opwindend.html>opwindender</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">opwindendst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>exciting, thrilling, exhilarating
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>Soms</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saai.html>saai</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>soms</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:opwindend.html>opwindend</a></b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Life <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> like that! Sometimes boring, sometimes exciting!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opwindend.html>opwindend</a></strong>

<p>From the voiced Verner alternant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ausô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ows-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_18">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>ear</li></ol>
</body>

***orakel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orakel.html>orakel</a> (11418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ōrāculum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orakel.html>orakel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orakels.html>orakels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orakelen.html>orakelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orakel.html>orakeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">oracle</span>
<ol><li>prophetic message, typically formulated in vague <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></li>
<li>shrine dedicated to a deity where such messages are given</li>
<li>person who formulates such messages</li></ol></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oranje.html>oranje</a> (4878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">arance</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">orange</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">orenge</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">arange</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">arancia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Spanish">Old Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp">naranja</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">نَارَنْج</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nāranj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">نارنگ</i> | , from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">नारङ्ग</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nāraṅga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dravidian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Dravidian languages">Dravidian</a></span>.
</p><p>The spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> subsequently influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">orange</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a> (89675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tun, cask; whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, see there for more. Although the origin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> obscure, the sometimes-cited association with <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">orcus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">underworld</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> folk-etymology.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">orcas</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sea mammal (<i>Orcinus <a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></i>) related to <a href = vnd.unilang:dolphins.html>dolphins</a> and porpoises, commonly called the killer whale.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">grampus</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">killer whale</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">blackfish</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orde.html>orde</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ordelijk.html>ordelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ordelijk.html>ordelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ordelijkst</b>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">organe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">organum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄργανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">órganon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***orkaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orkaan.html>orkaan</a> (5568)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">huracán</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" class="extiw" title="w:Taíno language">Taíno</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tnq">juracán</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">ouragan</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hurricane</i> (originally <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hurricano</i>); <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Orkan</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orkaan.html>orkaan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orkanen.html>orkanen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orkaan.html>orkaantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hurricane</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An uncontrollable/destructive force</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something moving extremely fast</li></ol>
